Tariff management

CARDS-56728

Added a new check for the uniqueness of the "Tariff Code Ext" field (tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM) in a personal domain when approving a personal tariff. If several tariffs with the same "Tariff Code Ext" are found in the same personal tariff domain, an error message with the text "There is more than one tariff with TariffCodeExt = %%" will be returned.
Upgrade Note:
The system configuration must be checked using preliminary script for the presence of a non-unique value for the tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM (Tariff Code Ext) field in the tariff domain. If this is the case, the codes must be given unique values.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-56728_TARIFF_table_code_from_uniqueness.sql
Updated Manuals: [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

CARDS-60213

Fixed OVL_THRESHOLD tariff behaviour when a personal tariff is used for the top issuing contract with affiliated subcontracts.
Upgrade Note:
If OVL_THRESHOLD is defined as a personal tariff for the top contract in a hierarchy, it will be applied for all contracts downward, even those which are linked to the top contract with Affiliated/Only Reporting types of liability links.
To use a personal OVL_THRESHOLD for the top level contract only, without affecting the available amount of Affiliated/Only Reporting liability subcontracts, the value PERS_DOMAIN_LEVEL=CURRENT; should be defined in the "Search Rules" field for the OVL_THRESHOLD tariff type.
Updated Manuals: [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf] [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

Transaction management

CARDS-55877

Added new API procedure doc_api.CHECK_DOC_RO which allows to check a document record before inserting it into the database. The procedure calls the standard document processing checks and generates the same return code as if this document was inserted into the database.
Upgrade Note:
When the new mode for checking documents is supported (without inserting a document into the database), custom logic used in the document check procedure must be corrected (CUST_ACCEPT_DOC_BEFORE, CUST_ACCEPT_DOC_AFTER, CUST_DOC_TARGET, CUST_DOC_SOURCE, CUST_CHECK_DOC_AMOUNT procedures and some others). 
In the new mode, a document is processed with the parameter OnlyCheck=Y and a document record's ID that is equal to 0 (zero). In this case, no inserts or updates are made for this document.
Use of the srcd.SET_DOC_ERROR function is not allowed as it requires a document to be inserted into the database. The srcd.SET_DOC_ERROR_R function working with a document record must be used instead.

CARDS-55773

Optimized BIN table record search. If a BIN record is found, no further search of BIN records with a wider sub bin is performed. This behaviour can be disabled by setting the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=N (the default value is "Y"). A Check action has been added to the form for BIN table records with "Own" data source.
Upgrade Note:
BIN table configuration should be checked for records with the "Own" data source using the preliminary check script. The script should be run and data should be fixed before upgrading to the new version of Cards. The script results will be written in the Process Log under the "Validate own BIN records" process. 
If BIN records with a wider (fewer digits) Sub BIN have a higher BIN group level or priority than records with a narrower Sub BIN (more digits), they will not be found in a BIN table search if the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=Y (default value). In this case, a BIN record should be reconfigured to have a Sub BIN with the same number of digits as other records, or even more (the maximum supported Sub BIN length is 6 digits).
Check Scripts:
CARDS-55773_own_bins.sql

CARDS-56435

Revised BIN record and routing search for foreign cards on document accept. Search will now be made using both "Target Member ID" and "Target Number", instead of searching by "Target Number" only.
Upgrade Note:
Since the routing search method for foreign cards on document accept has changed and now checks "Member ID" in addition to BIN range for the card, configured Own BIN records should be checked that they contain the correct member IDs corresponding to BIN ranges.
Updated Manuals: [transaction_management\Documents.pdf]

CARDS-56713

Processing of standard tags that could be configured in the "Custom Rules" field of the "Interchange Routing" table is moved from the custom procedure CUST_ROUTE_ENABLED to the standard code. The standard custom procedure is now empty and contains no checks.
Upgrade Note:
Processing of standard tags that could be configured in the "Custom Rules" field of the "Interchange Routing" table is moved from the custom procedure to the standard code.
The following tags are now processed in the standard code:
BIN_COUNTRY, REGION_FOR_ISSUER, PRODUCT_ID, BIN_AREA, MRC_COUNTRY, MRC_AREA, and MRC_EQ_BIN_COUNTRY.
Processing of tags listed above should be excluded from the customised procedure CUST_ROUTE_ENABLED.

Added the PS_REF_NUMBER and RET_REF_NUMBER fields to the DOC_TARGET_SOURCE index in the DOC table.
Upgrade Note:
DOC_TARGET_SOURCE index has been altered, the index will be rebuilt on upgrade, which may be a lengthy process.

CARDS-55318 / I1710032010

Changed the default value of the BLOCK_DISTRIBUTED_LIMIT global parameter to "N".
Upgrade Note:
By default, credit limit document posting will not affect the source bank contract. It is done to avoid deadlocks on bank contract during massive credit limit document posting. If a credit limit should be reflected in the source bank contract, the BLOCK_DISTRIBUTED_LIMIT parameter should be set to "Y".
Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]

CARDS-58520

Eliminated attempts to fill BIN record reference on document accept and other card related checks for non-card contracts. The target contract's contract category is now checked instead of the transaction type's contract category.
Upgrade Note:
AUTH_TYPE and PAN document tags are no longer filled for mVisa payments. If the AUTH_TYPE tag was used to identify mVisa payments in product settings (e.g. services or usages), other distinguishing characteristic should be chosen (e.g. the BAI tag) and corresponding settings should be changed.

CARDS-58531

Removed multiple error messages if the "Approve" or "Accept" actions are performed for a document when the source number is missing. No search will be made for transaction authorisations with the "Interbank" and "Settlement" transaction types even if the "Is Authorized" field in the transaction type setup is set to "Always" or "May Be".
Upgrade Note:
Check that the "Is Authorized" field for the "Interbank" and "Settlement" transaction types is set to "Never". Use a check script to determine whether there is a transaction type that must be reconfigured.
Check Scripts:
CARDS-58531_impersonal_authorized_transtypes.sql

CARDS-59489

Corrected fee amount calculation that was using the mtr.CRE_TEST_MTR procedure to work on secondary nodes of a high availability configuration.
Upgrade Note:
The procedure mtr.CRE_TEST_MTR will not raise an exception when executed on a secondary node of a high availability configuration. Custom code should be checked so that macrotransactions returned by the CRE_TEST_MTR procedure are not inserted into the database.

CARDS-55740

Increased the length of the fields DOC.REASON_CODE, DSP_REASON.CODE, REASON_CODE.CODE, REASON_ACTION.TGT_REASON_CODE, DISPUTE_TYPE.INW_REASON_CODE, DISPUTE_TYPE.REASON_CODE, DISPUTE_ITEM.INW_REASON_CODE, DISPUTE_ITEM.REASON_CODE, CM_CASE_DOC.REASON_CODE from 4 to 32 symbols.
Upgrade Note:
This change was made to support VISA Claim Resolution requirements. Long values for custom Reason Codes can only be used for VCR purposes. All custom interfaces that might export/import VISA dispute documents should support long Reason Code values.
The corresponding views are also impacted and they should be synchronised.

VISA interface

CARDS-54827

Enhanced determination of the IPS Member Identifier (Member_ID) for account contracts (statistical contract groups for account contracts). Now Member_ID is calculated as Member_ID of the card contracts subordinate to the account contract while before Member_ID was calculated based on the interchange routing settings.
Supported an optional IPS Member Identifier set up for reporting purposes:
- The ability to define Acquiring/Issuing Member ID by IPS.
- The ability to aggregate reporting data that belong to different financial institutions under the same Member ID.
- The ability to report financial institution data with the different Member IDs by Issuing BINs.
Added the new menu item OpenWay\Full\Statistics\Dictionaries\Payment Scheme Identification.
For more details, please refer to the OW_HOME\manuals\language\MasterCard_statistical_reports\Quarterly_MasterCard_Reporting\MC_Statistical_Reports.pdf,
 OW_HOME\manuals\language\VISA_statistical_reports\Quarterly_Operating_Certificates\VISA_Statistical_Reports.pdf,
 OW_HOME\manuals\language\AMEX_statistical_reports\AMEX_statistical_reports.pdf.
Upgrade Note:
Determination of the IPS Member Identifier (Member_ID) for account contracts (statistical contract groups for account contracts) has been corrected to avoid inconsistencies in data. Now Member_ID is calculated as Member_ID of the card contracts that are subordinate to the account contract while before Member_ID was calculated based on the interchange routing settings. 
Previous system behaviour is no longer supported. For more details, please refer to the following documentation: OW_HOME\manuals\language\MasterCard_statistical_reports\Quarterly_MasterCard_Reporting\MC_Statistical_Reports.pdf,

CARDS-55114

Modified the XLS_Visa_Statistics_Issuing_Business.rdf report. Now "Number of Statements Mailed" and "Number of Statements Mailed with Finance Charges" are gathered only for card categories with the parent value of card programme = "CREDIT" (DWD_CARD_CATEGORY classifier values with the "Parent value"="CREDIT") and multiplied on billing cycles number.

- P_FILTER_11
- P_FILTER_12

CARDS-55831

Synchronized the name "WSP_REQ_ID" of the document tag representing the "Token Requestor ID" field supported in "TCR4 - Supplemental Financial Data" in BASE II Draft Data Transactions with the name of the same tag stored as the document tag representing the token "Requestor ID" parameter. Renamed the "WSP_TKNREQID" tag to "WSP_REQ_ID".
Upgrade Note:
Incorrect naming of the "Token Requestor ID" tag in online documents has been fixed.
The "WSP_REQ_ID" tag is filled in according to the "TCR4 - Supplemental Financial Data" field in BASE II Draft Data" for uploaded documents, for online documents the value of the "Token Requestor ID" field was stored in the "WSP_TKNREQID" tag.
Names have been synchronized, the tag name for online documents has been changed from "WSP_TKNREQID" to "WSP_REQ_ID". 
It is necessary to check whether the "WSP_TKNREQID" tag is used in any applications. 
If so, it should be renamed to "WSP_REQ_ID".

CARDS-55951

Added the ability to process (import and export) VCR status advices via the UFX H2H interface.
Upgrade Note:
Added the ability to export and to import advices for "outgoing" transactions (for example VISA VCR advices for originator of transaction) via the UFX H2H Interface ("IC Documents Import" and "IC Documents Export" pipes with MODE=H2H pipe parameter set).

To avoid duplicates, exported records are marked with the "H2H_SENT=Y;" document tag. The recommended additional condition for the FILTER pipe parameter to export such transactions is "doc.source_channel = <Aff channel> and doc.target_channel = 'V' and doc.outward_status = 'C' and doc.fx_settl_date beetwen (<date1>,<date2>)". For correct export of advices for "outgoing" transactions, additional settings of the current menu items used for H2H document export (IC Documents Export pipe) are required:

If a menu item has FILE_SENDER and FILE_RECEIVER pipe parameters explicitly set as a constant value (not as an sql expression) then the FILTER pipe parameter of the existing menu item should be modified as specified above.

If FILE_SENDER and FILE_RECEIVER parameters are not set (the default values are DOC.SEND_MEMBER_ID and DOC.TARGET_MEMBER_ID respectively) or they are set as another sql expression it is recommended to create a separate menu item with FILE_SENDER=DOC.REC_MEMBER_ID and FILE_RECEIVER=DOC.SOURCE_MEMBER_ID parameters. The FILTER pipe parameter described above should be also added to the pipe in the new menu item.

Note that the proposed settings are recommended and are subject to testing on a particular WAY4 system configuration. Contact Customer Support if any obstacles are encountered during the testing.

No additional settings are needed for the "IC Documents Import" pipe to import advices for "outgoing" transactions.
Updated Manuals: [UFX_H2H_Interchange.pdf (NDA Specification for vendors)]

CARDS-60304

Supported new processing rules for transactions with deferred authorization in VISA and Affiliated BASE II inward and outward pipes. 
The new message reason code value of 5206 (Deferred authorization) will be saved to the VISA_MRC tag on posting or inward processing. The transaction attribute DEFERRED will be set for such financial documents too. 
Pipes affected:
Affiliated BASEII Outward Processing.dll, Affiliated BASEII Prepared Outward Processing.dll, Visa Base II Outward Processing.dll, VISA BASEII ONUS Marked Outward Processing.dll, VISA BASEII ONUS Outward Processing.dll, VISA BASEII Prepared Outward Processing.dll.
VISA BASEII Inward Processing.dll, Affiliated VISA BASEII Inward Processing.dll

Packages affected:
stl_b.sql
tr_cond_b.sql

Procedure affected:
cust_mark_onus.sql
Upgrade Note:
Changed the format of returned values in the functions tr_cond.get_visa_ta and get_visa_ta_f. Now these functions return a tagged string, VISA_TA=<value>; the tag VISA_MRC=5206 is added at the end for deferred documents.
Due to the change in the format of returned values in these functions, the cust_mark_onus function code has changed. 
Required settings to activate this behaviour are described in the 2019_04_VISA_Requirements.pdf standard manual.
Updated Manuals: [ips_releases\visa\20XX_XX_VISA_Requirements.pdf]

CARDS-56502 / I1710317086

Changed the VISA_FAST_FUNDS additional global parameter default value from the existing value "Y" to a new value "A". If VISA_FAST_FUNDS is set to "A", all original credit transactions will be converted into notifications regardless of the Fast Funds Indicator value. For all other transactions, the processing logic remains unchanged. The changes affect the VISA Base II Inward Processing and Affiliated Base II Inward Processing pipes. Please see CUN for required additional actions.
Upgrade Note:
A new default value ("A") has been added for the existing global parameter VISA_FAST_FUNDS. If VISA_FAST_FUNDS="A", all Original Credit Transactions being loaded will be converted to NotifItem, regardless of the Fast Funds Indicator value. For other documents, processing logic remains the same as VISA_FAST_FUNDS="Y". To restore the pipe's previous behaviour, the VISA_FAST_FUNDS parameter value must be set to "Y". It's recommended to have VISA_FAST_FUNDS="A" if Fast Funds authoirization request messages are processed as Financial Credit.

e-Commerce issuing

Fixed automatic creation of authentication schemes on demand.
Upgrade Note:
If 3-D authentication must automatically be available for all a bank's clients, the authentication type TDS_ENROLL must be explicitly included in the TDE domain, in the same way as other authentication types required. Ensure this setup has been made before upgrade.

Pipe affected:

    • [CARDS-62259]
      • Added the restriction on a new instalment scheme for the "Change Instalment Terms" action. The new scheme must have the same "Invoice Code" as the current scheme.
To enable the selection of an instalment scheme with the different invoice code, the INST_ALLOW_CODE_CHANGE global parameter should be set to "Y" (can be redefined in financial institution). The default parameter value is "N", that is the invoice code cannot be changed.
      Upgrade Note:
      The default behaviour of the "Change Instalment Terms" action has been changed. Now selecting an instalment scheme with the invoice code different from that of the current instalment plan scheme is restricted by default. To enable the old behaviour, the INST_ALLOW_CODE_CHANGE global parameter must be set to "Y" (can be redefined in financial institution).
Note that if changing invoice code is enabled, invoice Events and standing payment orders to transfer funds to appropriate accounts must be configured.
      Updated Manuals: Instalment management | Instalments

    • [CARDS-57816]
      • Added the ability to convert an authorisation to instalment from the "Auth" link in the "Instalment Contract Data" form. An instalment plan status is set according to the INST_APPROVE_PLANS parameter. 
If INST_APPROVE_PLANS=Y, the plan is assigned the "Preview" status. After approval or if INST_APPROVE_PLANS=N the plan status becomes "Inactive" and awaits of financial document posting. After a financial document has been posted, the instalment plan is activated or recalculated according to the INST_FIN_ACTION parameter. New custom function CUST_INSTL_ACTION is called during financial document posting that makes it possible to define what to do with the instalment plan if some attributes of the financial document differ from the authorisation.
      Upgrade Note:
      The behaviour of instalment plan activation in the "Preview" status has been changed during financial document posting. If the parameter INST_APPROVE_PLANS=Y is configured, an instalment plan in the "Preview" status linked to an authorisation document will not be approved. The plan will be just relinked to the financial document and will require manual approval.
      Updated Manuals: Instalment management | Instalments

    • [CARDS-61494]
      • Corrected the CLOSE_IF_EMPTY%-statement processing: registration in balance type table is mandatory for user balance types and is not required for hardcoded balance types.
      Upgrade Note:
      Use the script CARDS-61494_event_type.sql to find balance types which are not registered in the system (including hardcoded balance types) but are specified in the tags "CLOSE_IF EMPTY" and "CLOSE_IF EMPTY_LIAB" for Events. Analyse the records returned by the script and change settings, if necessary:
- Custom balance types must be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary if they must be checked when closing an Event; otherwise, they must be excluded from Event type settings.
- For hardcoded balances, system behaviour has changed: now balance types will always be checked when processing the corresponding Events (hardcoded balance types do not have to be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary). Previously, if hardcoded balance types were not registered in the the "Balance Type" dictionary, they were not checked when closing an Event.
      Check Scripts:
      CARDS-61494_event_type.sql

If there are any Warnings in process messages, note that behaviour when a card is reissued with the same product might be changed due to this fix.     • [CARDS-52181]
      • The DCC_CONTRACT tag is checked during Nostro contract approve; it should be the same for Main and Sub Nostro contracts. When searching for the DCC_CONTRACT tag in Nostro contracts, the tag is first searched for in the Sub Nostro contract, then in the Main Nostro contract, and then on the Nostro Account Scheme. Earlier, the DCC_CONTRACT tag value in the Main Nostro contract was not considered.
      Upgrade Note:
      Clients using Dynamic Currency Conversion (DCC) or Multi Currency Pricing (MCP/MCA) products must perform a check using CHECK_v1_CARDS-52181_dcc_contract_numbers.sql script validating the settings of DCC_CONTRACT tags in NOSTRO contracts. If the check returns a non-empty number of strings, a detailed check must be performed and the results of both checks must be sent to Customer Support.

      • Added new report parameters in the "XLS_MC_Statistics_Acquiring_Business" report:
P_FILTER_ACT_MRCH, varchar2(4000), default value is c.is_active_year = 1. The parameter defines additional conditions for the "Number of Mastercard Merchants" and "Total merchant locations" report metrics. The default value is "device has transaction activity for last year".

P_FILTER_ACT_CASH, varchar2(4000), default value is 1=1. The parameter defines additional conditions for the "Number of branch locations where cash can be obtained", "Number of ATMs", and "Number of Mastercard-approved EMV chip compliant ATMs accepting Mastercard cards" report metrics.

P_FILTER_ACT_POS, varchar2(4000), default value is c.is_active_year = 1. The parameter defines additional conditions for the "Number of POS terminals at your merchant locations", "Number of Merchant Locations with MasterCard-approved EMV Chip terminals accepting MasterCard cards", "Number of MasterCard-approved EMV chip terminals (with or without PIN pad) at your merchant locations", "Number of MasterCard-approved EMV chip terminals(with a PIN pad) at your merchant locations", "Number of merchant locations with MasterCard-approved PayPass terminals accepting MasterCard cards", and "Number of MasterCard-approved PayPass terminals at your merchant locations" report metrics.

    • [CARDS-60347]
      • Supported the reserving rules announced by the Central Bank of Russia based on International Financial Reporting Standards (IFRS). The rules become mandatory starting from 01.01.2019. According to these rules, reserves for the same debt must be created twice (standard reserves and difference between the standard and IFRS reserves) and simultaneously. The rules make it possible to move reserves between the reserve account in case of delinquency
The functionality is provided by Implementation Project.
      Upgrade Note:
      During the upgrade, the "Event Group Code" field's value for Reserving Schemes can be modified. The "Event Group Code" field will be filled in with the value of the "Group Code" field for an Event type that is set in the "Accrual Code" field for the Reserving Scheme.These changes do not impact the standard Reserving configuration, but may affect some specific and custom solutions. It is recommended to check custom menu items and procedures if they use the "Event Group Code" field of the Reserving Schemes and correct them accordingly.

    • [WM-3296]
      • Changed digital signature algorithm to SHA-512 for WAY4 Remote Access distributives (new installations and updates).
      Upgrade Note:
      To switch to the SHA-512 algorithm, reissue and reinstall the server application and all client applications.
To ensure operation is not interrupted during upgrade, it is recommended to do the following:
- For applications that have already been configured, issue a new update after WAY4 Cards has been updated.
- To gradually switch to the new algorithm for applications that have already been configured and new client applications, create a new application (Add new Application...) and new node (Nodes->Add...) with its own URL (internet_url). Export and install the new server application. Export and distribute the new client application for installation.
- After all client applications have been reinstalled, the old application with an old node can be deleted.
    • [CARDS-59236]
      • Changed the algorithm for calculation of the fee amount for blocking on Issuing authorization. The target fee amount from the authorization document is used now as the fee amount of the main service. If it is absent, it will be recalculated according to the Target Service configuration. Previously, it was always recalculated, even if the document already had Fee Amount information. These changes do not impact standard Issuing Authorization, as it does not have any predefined Fee Amounts, but may affect some specific and custom solutions.
      Upgrade Note:
      It is necessary to check if configurations exist in which the actual fee amount that is specified in a document's "Target Fee Amount" field is blocked for the contract according to a custom fee under the main Service. The custom fee has the field value "Fee Percentage" = 100% and "<AUTH>" and "TGTFD" tags in the "Service Details" field. To check for problematic configurations, use the check script CARDS-59236_DOC_FEE_AMOUNT_01.sql.
If problems are found, contact Customer Support.
      Check Scripts:
      CARDS-59236_DOC_FEE_AMOUNT_01.sql

    • [I1807186129]/[CARDS-59585]
      • Corrected calculation of the following report fields in the XLS_MC_Statistics_Issuing_Business report for the "Account and Cards" section:

- "Accounts at the beginning of Quarter - Open" - now counts valid account contracts that have at least one valid card contract at the beginning of the reporting period.
- "Accounts at the beginning of Quarter - Blocked" - now counts account contracts that are blocked but have open/blocked cards, or account contracts that are valid but have blocked cards.

- "New accounts obtained during the quarter" - now counts new account contracts that are valid or blocked at the end of reporting period and have open/blocked cards.

- "Accounts at the end of quarter - Open" - now counts valid account contracts that have at least one valid card contract at the end of the reporting period.
- "Accounts at the end of Quarter - Blocked" - now counts account contracts that are blocked but have open/blocked cards, or account contracts that are valid but have blocked cards.

- "New cards obtained during quarter" - now counts new card contracts that were added in the reporting period and are valid or blocked at the end of the quarter.
      Updated Manuals: [mastercard_statistical_reports\quarterly_mastercard_reporting\MC_Statistical_Reports.pdf]

    • [I1808153593]/[CARDS-59336]
      • Changed default menu items for importing and exporting transactions to NSPK in Mastercard IPM format according to NSPK operational bulletin #43.2018.
      Upgrade Note:
      Clients in Russia that process Mastercard transactions should review menu items for importing and exporting these transactions to NSPK.

Inward Processing: if the "FILE_FORMAT" pipe parameter in the menu item for importing IPM files is absent or has the value "U1014", additional actions are not required. If "FILE_FORMAT" has the "RDW" value, it should be deleted before the first import of a file in 1014 blocked format.

Outward Processing: if the "FILE_FORMAT" pipe parameter in menu items for exporting IPM files (including Collection only files) is absent or has the value "U1014", additional actions are not required. If "FILE_FORMAT" has the "RDW" value, it should be deleted before the first export of a file in 1014 blocked format. Also if the menu item has a subitem for conversion from RDW to 1014 blocked format, this subitem shoud be deleted and the "IPMMAST__INITIAL_DIR" pipe parameter must be reviewed. It should contain the final (not temporary) directory.

Note that exported files must be sent to Mastercard also (not only to NSPK) according to "Mastercard Bulletin No.4 3 May 2016" as earlier. Since now NSPK and Mastercard formats match each other, there is no need to generate 2 files. A copy of the NSPK file can be sent to Mastercard.

    • [CARDS-58740]
      • Supported the ISO20022 Acceptor-to-Acquirer protocol (submitted by NEXO). The protocol provides an interaction between card payment Acceptors and Acquirers as a next generation international card payment standard which is dedicated to replace ISO 8583 including its various derivatives. The use of the protocol is acceptable to transport payment associated information directly from merchants as well as via a service provider intermediary content.

    • [CARDS-59084]
      • Added the ability to convert an authorisation to instalment from the "Auth" link in the "Instalment Contract Data" form. An instalment plan status is set according to the INST_APPROVE_PLANS parameter. 
If INST_APPROVE_PLANS=Y, the plan is assigned the "Preview" status. After approval or if INST_APPROVE_PLANS=N the plan status becomes "Inactive" and awaits of financial document posting. After a financial document has been posted, the instalment plan is activated or recalculated according to the INST_FIN_ACTION parameter. New custom function CUST_INSTL_ACTION is called during financial document posting that makes it possible to define what to do with the instalment plan if some attributes of the financial document differ from the authorisation.
      Upgrade Note:
      The behaviour of instalment plan activation in the "Preview" status has been changed during financial document posting. If the parameter INST_APPROVE_PLANS=Y is configured, an instalment plan in the "Preview" status linked to an authorisation document will not be approved. The plan will be just relinked to the financial document and will require manual approval.
      Updated Manuals: Instalment management | Instalments

    • [CARDS-56536]
      • Changed the source limits validation algorithm. When IRouter or the Issuer Authorisation module receives a message with Source Channel data and without the tag S_USG=CHECKED;, the module will validate source limits. See Upgrade Notes for details.
      Upgrade Note:
      System configuration should be revised by the customer to check for presence of potentially problematic configurations listed below:

- Limiters of Transaction/Credit types are configured for the source contract with the IPS. This source contract is used both for transactions made with "on us" cards (own authorisation) and "foreign" bank agent's cards (transit authorisation).

- Limiters of Transaction/Credit types are configured for the source contract with the affiliated bank. This source contract is used both for transactions made with "on us" cards (own authorisation for requests from affiliated bank's devices) and "foreign" cards (transit authorisation).

- Limiters configured not directly for a source contract but for a financial institution's liability contract should also be considered.

Previously, in such configurations, limiters were checked for transit authorisation only. In doing so, credit limiters count debit transactions and transaction limiters count credit transactions. Now limiters are checked for own authorisation as well. In doing so, credit limiters count credit transactions and transaction limiters count debit transactions.

Contact Customer Support if problematic configurations are found.

    • [CARDS-54344]
      • Enhanced Due Date calculation for due normalization for Payment Due (Long Payment Due) accounts. For ageing reclassification (WAIVED_PD threshold) Due Date for target account is now calculated as:
- current Due Date, if due normalization has not yet been performed for account,
- next Due Date, if due normalization has already been performed for account.

For due normalization between Payment Due (Long Payment Due) accounts with the same due settings, Due Date for the target account is now calculated as next cycle Due Date. It avoids transferring the amount to the deepest overdue bucket.
      Updated Manuals: [product_management\Client_Messages.pdf]

    • [CARDS-54550]
      • Enhanced due normalization for accounts with Due Type = "Contract Due" when the calculated date is a holiday according to the business calendar defined in the Account Scheme or Financial Institution, and when every calendar day is opened with the Contract Daily Updates process. In this case, Due normalization will be performed on the first working day after the holidays according to this business calendar. For due normalization, it is not recommended to use Functional Dates which may be a holiday. It is recommended to shift the resulting date to a working day.

      The customised fields processing has been fixed for MasterCard CDF Export process. If a customised field in the ADD_FIELDS_XX pipe parameters had [null] value, non-customised value was used for export. Now standard value is used only when there is no customised field in the ADD_FIELDS_XX pipe parameters. Otherwise, a customised value is used even if it has [null] value. Please review ADD_FIELDS_XX pipe parameters to check if [null] value ("<CustomField>=;") is used to export the non-customised fields.

    • [I1710242596]/[CARDS-57241]
      • Renamed the "Additional Text" to "Additional Info" field in "Case Configuration -> Activities -> System Actions".
      Upgrade Note:
      The "Additional Info" field of the "System Action" screen in the "Activities" menu is tagged field but it is used as text field. It is recommended to change the format of this field to the tagged. This allows to show this field correctly in the "System Actions" screen of the "Activities" menu on Way4Web platform in the following workbenches: Application Case Configuration, Dispute Case Configuration, Risk Case Configuration, Document Workflow Configuration, and Collection Case Configuration. 
To search for the records with data in the "Additional Info" field, select as follows: 

select * from cm_sys_action where amnd_state = 'A' and add_txt is not null 

The "COMMENT" tag must be added manually to the data with comment. Example of this field: COMMENT=Test Comment;.
Note that the size of the "Additional Info" field is Varchar2(4000) and must be considered when adding the "COMMENT" tag. 
For more information about standard tags in this field, see the document "Case Management Configuration".

    • [I1802068851]/[CARDS-56852]
      • Added the ability to convert incoming "fast funds" payments to notifications in UFX Import pipe in "H2H" mode.
      Upgrade Note:
      Added a new pipe parameter, FF_CODES_MAP which makes it possible to convert "fast funds" financial messages to notifications. If an incoming message contains the parameter FAST_FUNDS=Y in the AddInfo field, a message code will be substituted according to the FF_CODES_MAP parameter. FF_CODES_MAP has the following format: <OldMessageCode1>:<NewMessageCode1>,<RequestCategory1>;....<OldMessageCodeN>:<NewMessageCodeN>,<RequestCategoryN>; or the "N" value, which turns off message code substitution. The default value is "DpP--2X-:NpP--2S-,P;DpR--2X-:NpP--2S-,R;". To restore previous behaviour, the  "FF_CODES_MAP" pipe parameter value must be set to "N".
      Updated Manuals: [core_banking_interface\way4_ufx_interchange\UFX_Interchange.pdf]

    • [NET-140]/[CARDS-57867]
      • Changed the algorithm for creating client/contract address lists and logic for transliterating addresses so that addresses are no longer shown multiple times in WAY4 Web screens and in DB Manager/WAY4 Manager forms. See Client Upgrade Notes for additional information.
      Upgrade Note:
      The algorithm for defining a language for transliterating client or contract addresses has been changed so that addresses are no longer shown multiple times in WAY4 Web address screens and in the "Customer Service Screen" form in DB Manager/WAY4 Manager. 
Previously, to transliterate an address to English, WAY4 used a language specified for the client in case client address was used for the address_type by default (Default Address="Client Base Address" in "ROOT\OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Client Classifiers\Address Types") and there was no address with such address type in the CLIENT_ADDRESS table, 
or in case there was no CLIENT_ADDRESS at all (address was specified only in Client record) . 
The new behaviour is supported by additional global parameter USE_SYSTEM_ADDR_LANG with the "Y" value (default). 
Now WAY4 does not take client language into account, and in the aforementioned case uses the default system language from Global Constants. If language is not set for client or contract address, or it is set to English, or officer language is not defined, no transliteration for this address is performed.
The behaviour can be switched to use client language with additional global parameter USE_SYSTEM_ADDR_LANG set to "N" in case client address was used for the address_type by default and there was no address with such address type in the CLIENT_ADDRESS table, 
or in case there is no CLIENT_ADDRESS at all.

Now the client address list does not contain address specified in client record. The behaviour can be switched to the previous behaviour using additional global parameter USE_CL_BASE_ADDR with the "Y" value.

Logic for generating the list of addresses to show data in the WAY4 Web address screens and in the "Customer Service Screen" form in DB Manager/WAY4 Manager has been fixed:
1. If "Date To" of one address record equals to "Date From" of another address record with the same address type, WAY4 shows the latest created address record.
2. If the activation period of one address record overlaps the activation period of another address record with the same address type, WAY4 shows the address with fewer activation period.
      Updated Manuals: [core\Common_References_Books.pdf] [core\Global_Parameters.pdf] [] [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf]

    • [CARDS-58032]
      • Changed how the "Is Group Activity" field is filled in for an activity when the "ROOT\OpenWay\Case Management\Configuration Setup\Domain Configuration\Activities\Approve" action is executed.
Now the field's value is taken into account that was set manually by the user in "ROOT\OpenWay\Case Management\Configuration Setup\Domain Configuration\Activities\Details".
      Upgrade Note:
      The "Is Group Activity" field's value indicates whether this activity can be used simultaneously for a group of cases.
Previously, the value in this field set manually by the user was not taken into account when executing the "Approve" action for an activity. The "Yes" value was automatically set for all activities  that met the following conditions:
- The activity is not a system activity (IsSystem="No").
- A new case is not created when the activity is performed.
- An object is not added when the activity is performed.
- An object role is not specified for the activity.
- The activity is not a specific activity for the "D" (Dispute) domain category.
The "No" value was automatically set for all activities that did not meet the described conditions.

The algorithm of the "Approve" action that is automatically used to set the "No" value in the "Is Group Activity" field has been changed. Now the "No" value is only set for activities that meet at least one of the following conditions:
- It is a system activity (IsSystem="Yes").
- A new case is created when the activity is performed.
- An object is added when the activity is performed. A new object must be selected or created manually. For example, it is necessary to enter parameters of a new document.
The algorithm that is used to set the "Yes" value automatically has not been changed. All other activities that do not automatically change the value of the "Is Group Activity" field will have a value that was set manually by the user.

The old behaviour is not supported.
For activities that were configured previously, additional actions are not required.
      Updated Manuals: [case_management\Case_Management_Configuration.pdf]

    • [CARDS-54636]
      • Implemented  loading of historical data. Three new parameters have been added to the pipes com.openwaygroup.pipe.dci.clearing_import.jar and
com.openwaygroup.pipe.dci.inward_processing:
- HISTORY_MODE=Y/N (the default value is "N") - pipe's mode of operation.  If HISTORY_MODE=Y, data from an incoming file are loaded without addendums and with outward status="History" .
- HIST_ARN_LIST - ARN filter (list of ARN with commas as delimiters) for historical documents. The parameter only works if HISTORY_MODE=Y.  If the ARN of a processed document is included in this list, the document is downloaded. If HIST_ARN_LIST is empty and HISTORY_MODE =Y, all documents from the incoming file are downloaded as historical documents.
- HISTORY_POSTING=Y/N (the default value is "N"). If HISTORY_POSTING=Y, an attempt to post a downloadable document is made.

    • [CARDS-55951]
      • Added the ability to process (import and export) VCR status advices via the UFX H2H interface.
      Upgrade Note:
      Added the ability to export and to import advices for "outgoing" transactions (for example VISA VCR advices for originator of transaction) via the UFX H2H Interface ("IC Documents Import" and "IC Documents Export" pipes with MODE=H2H pipe parameter set).

To avoid duplicates, exported records are marked with the "H2H_SENT=Y;" document tag. The recommended additional condition for the FILTER pipe parameter to export such transactions is "doc.source_channel = <Aff channel> and doc.target_channel = 'V' and doc.outward_status = 'C' and doc.fx_settl_date beetwen (<date1>,<date2>)". For correct export of advices for "outgoing" transactions, additional settings of the current menu items used for H2H document export (IC Documents Export pipe) are required:

If a menu item has FILE_SENDER and FILE_RECEIVER pipe parameters explicitly set as a constant value (not as an sql expression) then the FILTER pipe parameter of the existing menu item should be modified as specified above.

If FILE_SENDER and FILE_RECEIVER parameters are not set (the default values are DOC.SEND_MEMBER_ID and DOC.TARGET_MEMBER_ID respectively) or they are set as another sql expression it is recommended to create a separate menu item with FILE_SENDER=DOC.REC_MEMBER_ID and FILE_RECEIVER=DOC.SOURCE_MEMBER_ID parameters. The FILTER pipe parameter described above should be also added to the pipe in the new menu item.

Note that the proposed settings are recommended and are subject to testing on a particular WAY4 system configuration. Contact Customer Support if any obstacles are encountered during the testing.

No additional settings are needed for the "IC Documents Import" pipe to import advices for "outgoing" transactions.
      Updated Manuals: [UFX_H2H_Interchange.pdf (NDA Specification for vendors)]

    • [CARDS-56155]
      • Changed JCB BIN Table Import pipe. Supported loading of new values from the "Card Product" field. Information about card product category (consumer/commercial) is stored in the "bin_table.product_category" database field in MasterCard notation ("1"-consumer, "2"-commercial, "4"-other). Also, the bin_table.licensed_product_id database field is filled with a 3-symbol product code (see the PDSE3001 field in the BIG manual for the list of possible values).
      Upgrade Note:
      Loading of new values from the "Card Product" field has been supported in the JCB BIN Table Import pipe. Information about card product category (consumer/commercial) is stored in the "bin_table.product_category" database field in MasterCard notation ("1"-consumer, "2"-commercial, "4"-other). Also, the "bin_table.licensed_product_id" database field is filled with a 3-symbol product code (see PDSE3001 field in the BIG manual for the list of possible values).  licensed_product_id is generated according to "Card Product" and "Card Grade" from an incoming IIN file. Two new pipe parameters have been added to generate licensed_product_id
- "MAP_PROD_TO_NAME" = "<product1>=<name_start1>;<product2>=<name_start2>;...<productn>=<name_startn>;", where <productx> - "Card Product" field from incoming IIN file and <name_startn> - first letter of the licensed_product_id. Default value "MAP_PROD_TO_NAME"="01=C;02=D;03=P;04=A;05=X;06=Y;"
- "MAP_GRADE_PROD_NAME" = "<grade1>=<name_end1>;<grade2>=<name_end2>;...<graden>=<name_end1>n", where <graden> - "Card Grade" field from incoming IIN file and <name_startn> - last 2 letters of the licensed_product_id. Default value "MAP_GRADE_PROD_NAME"="S=ST;G=GD;P=PL;R=PR;D=GR;E=EN;M=SP;U=UL;O=AL;"
No additional manual action is required.

    • [CARDS-55877]
      • Added new API procedure doc_api.CHECK_DOC_RO which allows to check a document record before inserting it into the database. The procedure calls the standard document processing checks and generates the same return code as if this document was inserted into the database.
      Upgrade Note:
      When the new mode for checking documents is supported (without inserting a document into the database), custom logic used in the document check procedure must be corrected (CUST_ACCEPT_DOC_BEFORE, CUST_ACCEPT_DOC_AFTER, CUST_DOC_TARGET, CUST_DOC_SOURCE, CUST_CHECK_DOC_AMOUNT procedures and some others). 
In the new mode, a document is processed with the parameter OnlyCheck=Y and a document record's ID that is equal to 0 (zero). In this case, no inserts or updates are made for this document.
Use of the srcd.SET_DOC_ERROR function is not allowed as it requires a document to be inserted into the database. The srcd.SET_DOC_ERROR_R function working with a document record must be used instead.

    • [I1702284414]/[CARDS-57558]
      • Implemented support for the Service Pack Approved entity in document processing. When the Service Pack has status is_ready = N or is approved from the future date, WAY4 will search for the actual data in the Service Pack Approved.
      Upgrade Note:
      Changed the default behaviour for all changes in the service_pack entities, except for Services: changing Special Parms field (auth_conf_mode), Service Events records, enabling/disabling additional Service Packages. 
Now changes occur starting from the "Date From" date of the [Approve] process. Previously the "Date From" value only affected Service Approved records.
Migration scripts for automatic filling of the table (Service Pack Approved) are not provided. Records in the new table (Service Pack Approved) will be created in real time during the service pack approval process.
If it is required to add changes to Service Package (additional or not) that was approved last time when WAY4 version was less than 03.46.30, do as follows:
1. Approve Service Package without any changes. To do so, any field of the Service Pack record must be changed to get "Not Ready" status in the is_ready field.
New SERVICE_PACK_APPROVED records will be created and Service Package editing will not affect transactions processing.
2. Make changes that were planned and approve Service Package with the date of changes.
3. Run the process "Apply Service Packs Changes" if required (if the global parameter APPROVE_IMMEDIATE=N).
    • [I1706150815]/[CARDS-58131]
      • Changed the default behaviour for switching on/off additional service packages.
Previously, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "No" was switched on manually for a contract, and then switched off again, this additional service package was permanently switched off. Even if the "Default Is Active" field subsequently changed to "Yes" for the service package. Likewise, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "Yes" was switched off manually for a contract, and then switched on again, this additional service package will be permanently switched on. Even if the "Default Is Active" field subsequently changed to "No" for the service package.
Now, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "No" was switched on manually for a contract, and then switched off again, this additional service package will use the service package's "Default Is Active" field. Therefore, if the "Default Is Active" field of the additional service package is changed to "Yes", it will be "Yes" for the contract. Likewise, when an additional service package with a "Default Is Active" field value of "Yes" was switched off manually for a contract, and then switched on again, this additional service package will use the service package's "Default Is Active" field. Therefore, if the "Default Is Active" field of the additional service package is changed to "No", it will be "No" for the contract.
      Upgrade Note:
      The configuration of products used in switching on/off additional service packages must be analysed to check if the new system behaviour corresponds to the expected result. In addition, note that now if DEFAULT_IS_ACTIVE = "Y" is set for an additional service package, changes will become effective from the approve date of the main service package (in previous versions, changes became effective immediately).
      Updated Manuals: [personal_data_management\Personal_Data_Management_Operational_Manual.pdf] [product_management\Service_Packages.pdf]

      • Changed how Case Management users are created by a template user. Now a Case Management user is created automatically only by an active template user. By default, a newly created user participates in automatic case routing.
      Upgrade Note:
      It is necessary to check that used template users are active. To do so, execute the query:

Select for finding not active users:
select d.name domain_name, g.name group_name, u.name user_name
  from cm_user u
  join cm_group g
    on u.cm_group__oid = g.id
  join cm_domain d on g.domain = d.id
 where u.amnd_state = 'A' and u.is_active = 'N'
   and u.user_type = 'TEMPLATE';

If any of the selected template users are used, it is necessary to set "Yes" in the Is Active field in the menu item "ROOT\OpenWay\Case Management\Configuration Setup\Users\Users".

    • [CARDS-51125]
      • Moved the Contract Parameters handbook to a separate table, CONTR_PARM. The obsolete handbook with Group Code CONTRACT_PARM_LIST is no longer supported.
      Upgrade Note:
      The method for storing the Contract Parameters handbook has changed. In this version, the form OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Common Handbooks\Contract Parameters Setup is based on the CONTR_PARM table, while in the previous version, the form showed data from the  SY_HANDBOOK table with the CONTRACT_PARM_LIST handbook code. When upgrading the version, a special update script is automatically executed that copies records from the old handbook to the new  CONTR_PARM table, fills in new fields, validates the new configuration that results, and changes the code of the old handbook in SY_HANDBOOK from CONTRACT_PARM_LIST to OLD_CONTRACT_PARM_LINK. 
The old handbook's data can be viewed in the form OpenWay\Full\DB Administrator Utilities\Special OpenWay Utilities\Product Utilities\OBSOLETE Contract Parameters handbook, however, they will not be processed.
The new Contract Parameters handbook contains several new functional fields, as well as the read-only field "Is Ready" that is set to "Yes" if this parameter is successfully validated. Validation is performed by an update script that can also be called by clicking on the [Check] button in the "Contract Parameters Setup" form. 
It is important to note that when moving data to new handbooks, the new field, "Sub Main Inheritance Rule" is filled in for contract parameters listed in the values of the global parameters TP_SUB_MAIN_INH and TP_SUB_MAIN_INH_EQUAL. These global parameters are then deleted and are no longer supported in WAY4.

After the new version has been installed, open the form OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Common Handbooks\Contract Parameters Setup and ensure that the "Is Ready" field contains "Yes" for all contract parameters that were moved.

It is important to note that collisions are possible when data are moved automatically. In this case, a record in the new handbook remains in the status Is Ready = No and requires analysis and manual correction.

Also note that when the Configuration Inspector module is used, it is possible that old configurations with data that were put into the obsolete Custom Handbook with the CONTRACT_PARM_LIST code can be loaded to WAY4. 
Starting with this version, regards the presence of records in the handbook with this code as an inconsistent configuration, which will cause errors when approving Products, Accounting Schemes, and Service Packages, and when checking financial institution settings.
When approving contracts, an error will not occur, but the following type of record will be generated in the Process Log:
"Obsolete Contract Parameters configuration for <N> parameters. It should be analyzed manually and either migrated or removed. See Upgrade Notes on Impact changes for CARDS-51125."

If the aforementioned errors are found during operation of the new WAY4 version, it is recommended to do as follows:
1. Open the form OpenWay\Full\DB Administrator Utilities\Special OpenWay Utilities\Product Utilities\OBSOLETE Contract Parameters handbook:
2. Filter data in it for the unsupported handbook with the  CONTRACT_PARM_LIST code. Records corresponding to this handbook are highlighted in red. Next, click on the [Check] button.
After the [Check] has been made, all the handbook's records that are duplicates of the new CONTR_PARM handbook will automatically be moved to the OLD_CONTRACT_PARM_LINK handbook.
3. Those records from the unsupported handbook, that are not duplicates of the new handbook will be marked either as New, or as Different in the Validation Flag column and the [Messages] button will be available for them to view the last messages on validation.
New records loaded to the old handbook can be added one-by-one to the new handbook by using the button [Actions] -> [Add to new Contract Parameters Setup] . Then, the CONTR_PARM handbook itself, the form (OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Common Handbooks\Contract Parameters Setup) must be validated again ([Check] button).
For records that differ from the new handbook (have the "Different" value in the "Validation Flag" column), all necessary changes must be entered manually in the new handbook. Then, the check can be repeated to move duplicates to the historic handbook. 
Or, when not all attributes of the old handbook must be move to the new one, after the check has been performed, WAY4 shows in Messages which of this parameter's attributes differ. If this meets expectations, the record in CONTRACT_PARM_LIST is forcibly moved to history, regardless of the differences. The button [Actions] -> [Remove] is used to do so.

When the "OBSOLETE Contract Parameters handbook" form contains records marked in red and it is not clear how to process them, it is recommended to contact Customer Support.
      Updated Manuals: [core\Contract_and_Client_Classifiers.pdf]

    • [CARDS-55429]
      • Supported 3 logging modes for the CS_DECISION_LOG table. Default behaviour has been changed.
      Upgrade Note:
      Changes have been made that impact configurations using Decisions.

To check for the existence of such a configuration, use the standard form: OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Common Handbooks\Decision.
If it is not empty, pay careful attention to the information below.

By default, logging of changes for all Decisions to the CS_DECISION_LOG table is disabled. This does cause any changes in processing, as this log is not used in processing. The current value of a Decision is always recalculated on the fly at the time it is asked.

Previously, logging of changes in Decisions was always deferred, using Object Task Scheduler, which sometimes resulted in a large queue of tasks for recalculating and logging the values of Decisions, although the CS_DECISION_LOG may not have been not used anywhere.

Disabling logging does not concern Decisions that are used in Datamart export. These decisions are always logged, regardless of any parameters. Only two log mode are possible for these Decisions: Deferred or Immediate (default).

Three log modes are now supported in WAY4:
1. SKIP - Don't log anything. Used by default for all Decisions, except those exported into Datamart.
2. DEFERRED - Deferred logging in CS_DECISION_LOG using Object Task Scheduler. This logging mode corresponds to the system's previous behaviour. Make sure that Object Task Scheduler is run regularly before enabling deferred log mode.
3. IMMEDIATE - Immediately recalculation and saving in CS_DECISION_LOG when a linked Classifier changes. This is used as the default mode for Decisions exported to Datamart. This mode is not recommended for Decisions that can be used for large contract trees, since a change in the value of a classifier in a hierarchy's top contract may cause immediate recalculation of dependent Decisions for all contracts in the hierarchy.

Log mode can be changed with the global parameter DECISION_LOG_MODE.
For the same behaviour for all Decisions (except those exported to Datamart), one of the aforementioned values should be used: SKIP or DEFERRED or IMMEDIATE.

To check logging mode for each Decision separately, use the value DECISION_LOG_MODE=CHECK_<Default Mode>, where Default Mode is a value: SKIP, DEFERRED, or IMMEDIATE. If the LOG_MODE tag is not set in a specific Decision, default mode will be used.

To set log mode for a Decision, use the LOG_MODE tag in the "Add Info" field. The mode in a specific decision is only checked when the global parameter has the value CHECK_<Default mode> and for Decisions used for export to Datamart.

If the CS_DECISION_LOG table is used in exports or custom processes, log mode should be changed according to these recommendations.
      Updated Manuals: [core\Contract_and_Client_Classifiers.pdf] [core\Global_Parameters.pdf] [tags description]

    • [CARDS-55773]
      • Optimized BIN table record search. If a BIN record is found, no further search of BIN records with a wider sub bin is performed. This behaviour can be disabled by setting the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=N (the default value is "Y"). A Check action has been added to the form for BIN table records with "Own" data source.
      Upgrade Note:
      BIN table configuration should be checked for records with the "Own" data source using the preliminary check script. The script should be run and data should be fixed before upgrading to the new version of Cards. The script results will be written in the Process Log under the "Validate own BIN records" process. 
If BIN records with a wider (fewer digits) Sub BIN have a higher BIN group level or priority than records with a narrower Sub BIN (more digits), they will not be found in a BIN table search if the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=Y (default value). In this case, a BIN record should be reconfigured to have a Sub BIN with the same number of digits as other records, or even more (the maximum supported Sub BIN length is 6 digits).

      • Added a new interest calculation scheme to configure an instalment scheme: "Interest with USE_MONTH_WEIGHT = B". In this configuration, interest for the first instalment portion is calculated for the whole month regardless of a number of days left to the end of the month. In case of early repayment, no advance interest is taken.
      Upgrade Note:

Now when an interest calculation scheme with the specified USE_MONTH_WEIGHT mode is selected on Instalment Scheme level, the USE_MONTH_WEIGHT tag in Account Scheme or Financial Institution is not checked at all.     • [I1712085785]/[CARDS-56635]
      • Changed the default behaviour of Events duplication when Contract is duplicated (reissued, etc.). Events with the "Waiting" status are now duplicated to a new contract along with Events with the "Posted", "Suspended", and "Inactive" statuses. Sometimes, Events with the "Waiting" status must not be duplicated to a new contract, for example, if they relate to the previous contract closing. These Events must be marked with the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE; tag.
      Upgrade Note:
      Event types that are used for reissuing card contracts and must not be duplicated to a newly created contract must be checked. The SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE; tag must be set for these Events. Previously, these Events were not duplicated to a new contract if they were in the "Waiting" status in the process of reissuing. Now the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE; tag must be set to avoid duplication of these Events. Otherwise, the Events will be duplicated to a new contract irrespective of the "Waiting" status, and the new contract may be closed, or other unwanted consequences may occur.

This updated behaviour is also applied to batch applications for Instalment management.
      Upgrade Note:
      Application Response contents have been changed for Instalment applications in online mode and in batch mode. The previous contents of a response (contract data returned) are no longer supported. This should be considered if Instalment applications are already used in the integration layer.
This change affects the following application types (see samples of file applications in manuals\english\application_management\file_samples\issuing\readme.txt):
- Add instalment by transaction                                              
- Update instalment                                                          
- Add instalment                                                             
- Partial EarlyRepayment instalment with KeepInstalmentNumber recalculation  
- Partial EarlyRepayment instalment with KeepInstalmentAmount recalculation  
- Full EarlyRepayment instalment                                             
- PaymentHolidays instalment                                                 
- Close instalment                                                           
New contents of the response message/file:
<DataRs>
  <InstalmentRs>
</DataRs>
Previous contents of the response message/file:
<DataRs>
  <ContractRs>
</DataRs>
    • [UFX-495]
      • Fixed incorrect behaviour on export of affiliated clients in UFX Information responses and in Changes Export pipe.
Affiliation/Code element in a UFX response is now filled with the value of affiliated_client.SOURCE_REG_NUMBER. Previously it was always the same as Affiliation/Type.
      Upgrade Note:
      Systems that expected Affiliation/Code to contain affiliation type code should be corrected to use Affiliation/Type instead.
The old behaviour is no longer supported.
    • [UFX-517]
      • Renamed elements from <StornoCorrection> to <Correction> and from <StornoDocId> to <CorrectionDocId> for UFX Additional Statement Request.
      Upgrade Note:
      Changes have been made in UFX Additional Statement Correction request. Elements have been renamed: from <StornoCorrection> to <Correction> and from <StornoDocId> to <CorrectionDocId>. The old field names cannot be used. <Correction> and <CorrectionDocId> must be used instead.
    • [DBK-3537]
      • Added the ability to specify the "BYSECOND" parameter for Health Monitoring background jobs with a repeat interval less than 86400 seconds.
      Upgrade Note:
      If autoswitchower monitoring jobs repeat interval is less than 60 seconds (default is 60) and you need to run the jobs synchronously on the different nodes you have to specify monitoring jobs repeat interval in the following way: repeat  interval must be a multiple of 60. For instance if you specify 20 it would be launched at 0, 20, 40 second
      Updated Manuals: [ultimate_ha\ha_auto_switchover\HA_Auto_Switchover_setup.pdf]
    • [WFCKF-3468]/[DBK-3397]
      • Changed Object Task Processing behaviour in case of SQL errors. Such tasks are moved to the "Suspended" status instead of the "Rejected" status.
All tasks with the same Table Code and Table Record Id will not be processed until this task is retried or rejected in the "Suspended Tasks" form.
      Upgrade Note:
      If Object Task Processing is used, Suspended tasks should be monitored in the "OpenWay\System\DB Administrator Utilities\Object Tasks\Suspended Tasks" form.
A Suspended task should be either retried or rejected.
      Updated Manuals: [ultimate_ha\ha_cluster\HA_Cluster_operation.pdf] [ultimate_ha\distributed_processing\Distributed_Processing_operation.pdf] [ultimate_ha\ha_switch\HA_Switch_operation.pdf] [ultimate_ha\Stand-in\Stand-In_operation.pdf]
    • [DBK-3167]
      • Fixed problem with Configuration Inspector which did not allow insertion of records into configuration tables after running "OpenWay\Copy Configuration\Copy Configuration Import Screen" -> [Data]-> [Import merged data] on WAY4 03.45.30.
      Upgrade Note:
      To fix configuration problems, run the OW_HOME\db\scripts\oracle\tools\synchseq.sql script after running "Configuration Import Screen\Data\Import Merged Data". It is only necessary to run the script if the configuration was imported to WAY4 versions between 03.45.30.00 and 03.45.30.32.
    • [DBK-3208]
      • Changed the pipe com.openwaygroup.pipe.write_audit_log_file.jar output to syslog (rfc5424) format.
      Upgrade Note:
      If data are exported from the sy_audit_log table (for more information, see the document "WAY4 Audit Log Export") to an external monitoring system, ensure the external monitoring system is ready to receive logs in syslog format.
Check for this pipe in the process log. Process name is PIPE: Audit Log Writing(com.openwaygroup.pipe.write_audit_log_file.jar).
      Check Scripts:
      Check script for this change is: DBK-3208_write_audit_log_file.sql. Script returns either "passed" (no action required) or "warning" if any action required.
    • [CARDS-57515]
      • Changed the default value of the "MC_PRC_TA" global parameter from "N" to "Y". This parameter manages if transaction attributes are calculated by special DB procedures ('Y" value) or by MC clearing pipes. Pipes affected: "IPM Outward Processing.dll", "IPM Inward Processing.dll"
      Upgrade Note:
      To restore the old behaviour, the "MC_PRC_TA" global parameter must be set to the "N" value.
      Updated Manuals: [core\Global_Parameters.pdf]
    • [CARDS-55999]
      • Supported new DE22.7 value "7" ("Credential-on-file") processing.
      Upgrade Note:
      New DE22.7 value "7" ("Credential-on-file") processing has been supported. Additional global parameter MC_RELEASE=18.Q3 must be set to export this new value to IPM file.
    • [WM-3099]
      • Upgrade Note:
      If conf/config.properties contains the copy_managed_jars attribute, it should be set according to the value present in system/config.properties. Application Server should be restarted after upgrading the server application.

Check Scripts Grouped by Products

There are following types of non-upgrade scripts: preliminary scripts (scripts show if customer has configuration or data, which will be impacted on new version), diagnostic scripts (scripts collect some configuration/data statistics).

For more information and description of the execution procedure, see the "WAY4 Upgrade" document (db_kernel\WAY4_Upgrade.pdf).

It is also recommended to check the configuration. Run the script CARDS-56042_Check_redef_channel_01.sql and send the result to Customer Support. This information is required for internal analysis of customer configurations for purposes of product development.

  • [I1804119098]/[CARDS-57800]

    Upgrade Note:
    The CODE field in the menu item "Case Management\Configuration Setup\Domain Configuration" must be filled in for the following objects: Case Parameters, Activity Reasons, Strategy, and Strategy Step. 
If the CODE field is not filled in, it is not possible to approve a strategy that was obtained by using the "Duplicate" action to copy an existing strategy.

To find objects with an empty CODE field, run check script .

    Issuing

  • [CARDS-61043]
    • Fixed the default classifier value assigned to a new card contract after reissuing with the same product and the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE classifier attribute. Correct behaviour - the classifier value for the new card should be taken from the default value defined for the Product, not the general default value for this classifier.
    Upgrade Note:
    The CARDS-61043_product_classifier.sql script is used to detect a problematic configuration in which a classifier with SetToContract = Yes or null and the SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE tag is set for the product. After running the script, check the Process Log for a process named "Checking product options with SKIP_FOR_DUPLICATE". If there are any Warnings in process messages, note that behaviour when a card is reissued with the same product might be changed due to this fix. If the new behaviour does not correspond to expectations, contact Customer Support with a detailed description of the required behaviour.
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-61043_product_classifier.sql
    Updated Manuals: [issuing\user_manuals\Issuing_Module.pdf]

    Issuing authorisation

  • [CARDS-59236]
    • Changed the algorithm for calculation of the fee amount for blocking on Issuing authorization. The target fee amount from the authorization document is used now as the fee amount of the main service. If it is absent, it will be recalculated according to the Target Service configuration. Previously, it was always recalculated, even if the document already had Fee Amount information. These changes do not impact standard Issuing Authorization, as it does not have any predefined Fee Amounts, but may affect some specific and custom solutions.
    Upgrade Note:
    It is necessary to check if configurations exist in which the actual fee amount that is specified in a document's "Target Fee Amount" field is blocked for the contract according to a custom fee under the main Service. The custom fee has the field value "Fee Percentage" = 100% and "<AUTH>" and "TGTFD" tags in the "Service Details" field. To check for problematic configurations, use the check script CARDS-59236_DOC_FEE_AMOUNT_01.sql.
If problems are found, contact Customer Support.
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-59236_DOC_FEE_AMOUNT_01.sql
  • [CARDS-59425]
    • Changed the algorithm for calculation of the fee amount for blocking on Issuing authorization.     Product management

  • [CARDS-55995]
    • Implemented forms for adding/editing product classifiers with "No" in the "Set to Contract" field; after changes made using the new forms it is not necessary to reapprove the product. Additionally, when approving a product, the value of the "Set to Contract" field value is automatically set with the SET_TO_CONTRACT tag value, if the tag is specified in the "Custom Rules" field of the "Product" -> [Classifiers] form, or with the "Yes" value, if this tag is not present.
    Upgrade Note:
    When approving a Product, a check is made of whether classifier date ranges overlap. If dates overlap, changes to a Product will not be approved, and the message "Incorrect intersection of activity periods of the classifier" will be displayed.
    Check Scripts:
    To detect overlapping dates for classifiers, use the test script CHECK_V2_CARDS-55995_product_classifiers.sql. The results of this script will be saved in the "Checking product options" process log. To fix overlapping periods, use the standard form "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Products\Product Definition\Products -> [Classifiers]".
    Updated Manuals: [core\Contract_and_Client_Classifiers.pdf] [product_management\Products_and_Subtypes.pdf]
  • [CARDS-61441]
    • Corrected calculation of Past Due date/Past Due days in CALC_PD_DATE mode, now calculation starts from the first overdue date, not the current due date.
    Upgrade Note:
    Run CARDS-61441_account_schemes_with_CALC_PD_DATE.sql to check whether CALC_PD_DATE mode is used or not.
If any records are selected, note that initially the Past Due date and number of days of delinquency were calculated starting from the date when Current Due balance appeared, and from the next Acc Scheme Approve and Apply Changes process - these values will be calculated starting from the date when Past Due balance appeared. If the new behaviour is not suitable, contact Customer Support with a detailed business case description.
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-61441_account_schemes_with_CALC_PD_DATE.sql
  • [CARDS-61494]
    • Corrected the CLOSE_IF_EMPTY%-statement processing: registration in balance type table is mandatory for user balance types and is not required for hardcoded balance types.
    Upgrade Note:
    Use the script CARDS-61494_event_type.sql to find balance types which are not registered in the system (including hardcoded balance types) but are specified in the tags "CLOSE_IF EMPTY" and "CLOSE_IF EMPTY_LIAB" for Events. Analyse the records returned by the script and change settings, if necessary:
- Custom balance types must be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary if they must be checked when closing an Event; otherwise, they must be excluded from Event type settings.
- For hardcoded balances, system behaviour has changed: now balance types will always be checked when processing the corresponding Events (hardcoded balance types do not have to be registered in the "Balance Type" dictionary). Previously, if hardcoded balance types were not registered in the the "Balance Type" dictionary, they were not checked when closing an Event.
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-61494_event_type.sql
    Updated Manuals: [product_management\Events.pdf]

    Tariff management

  • [CARDS-56728]
    • Added a new check for the uniqueness of the "Tariff Code Ext" field (tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM) in a personal domain when approving a personal tariff. If several tariffs with the same "Tariff Code Ext" are found in the same personal tariff domain, an error message with the text "There is more than one tariff with TariffCodeExt = %%" will be returned.
    Upgrade Note:
    The system configuration must be checked using preliminary script for the presence of a non-unique value for the tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM (Tariff Code Ext) field in the tariff domain. If this is the case, the codes must be given unique values.
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-56728_TARIFF_table_code_from_uniqueness.sql
    Updated Manuals: [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]

    Transaction management

  • [CARDS-55773]
    • Optimized BIN table record search. If a BIN record is found, no further search of BIN records with a wider sub bin is performed. This behaviour can be disabled by setting the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=N (the default value is "Y"). A Check action has been added to the form for BIN table records with "Own" data source.
    Upgrade Note:
    BIN table configuration should be checked for records with the "Own" data source using the preliminary check script. The script should be run and data should be fixed before upgrading to the new version of Cards. The script results will be written in the Process Log under the "Validate own BIN records" process. 
If BIN records with a wider (fewer digits) Sub BIN have a higher BIN group level or priority than records with a narrower Sub BIN (more digits), they will not be found in a BIN table search if the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=Y (default value). In this case, a BIN record should be reconfigured to have a Sub BIN with the same number of digits as other records, or even more (the maximum supported Sub BIN length is 6 digits).
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-55773_own_bins.sql
  • [CARDS-58531]
    • Removed multiple error messages if the "Approve" or "Accept" actions are performed for a document when the source number is missing. No search will be made for transaction authorisations with the "Interbank" and "Settlement" transaction types even if the "Is Authorized" field in the transaction type setup is set to "Always" or "May Be".
    Upgrade Note:
    Check that the "Is Authorized" field for the "Interbank" and "Settlement" transaction types is set to "Never". Use a check script to determine whether there is a transaction type that must be reconfigured.
    Check Scripts:
    CARDS-58531_impersonal_authorized_transtypes.sql

This behaviour can be disabled by setting the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=N (the default value is "Y"). A Check action has been added to the form for BIN table records with "Own" data source.
        Upgrade Note:
        BIN table configuration should be checked for records with the "Own" data source using the preliminary check script. The script should be run and data should be fixed before upgrading to the new version of Cards. The script results will be written in the Process Log under the "Validate own BIN records" process. 
If BIN records with a wider (fewer digits) Sub BIN have a higher BIN group level or priority than records with a narrower Sub BIN (more digits), they will not be found in a BIN table search if the global parameter SKIP_WIDER_BIN_SEARCH=Y (default value). In this case, a BIN record should be reconfigured to have a Sub BIN with the same number of digits as other records, or even more (the maximum supported Sub BIN length is 6 digits).
        Check Scripts:
        CARDS-55773_own_bins.sql
      • [CARDS-55995]
        • Implemented forms for adding/editing product classifiers with "No" in the "Set to Contract" field; after changes made using the new forms it is not necessary to reapprove the product. Additionally, when approving a product, the value of the "Set to Contract" field value is automatically set with the SET_TO_CONTRACT tag value, if the tag is specified in the "Custom Rules" field of the "Product" -> [Classifiers] form, or with the "Yes" value, if this tag is not present.
        Upgrade Note:
        When approving a Product, a check is made of whether classifier date ranges overlap. If dates overlap, changes to a Product will not be approved, and the message "Incorrect intersection of activity periods of the classifier" will be displayed.
        Check Scripts:
        To detect overlapping dates for classifiers, use the test script CHECK_V2_CARDS-55995_product_classifiers.sql. The results of this script will be saved in the "Checking product options" process log. To fix overlapping periods, use the standard form "OpenWay\Full\Configuration Setup\Products\Product Definition\Products -> [Classifiers]".
        Updated Manuals: [core\Contract_and_Client_Classifiers.pdf] [product_management\Products_and_Subtypes.pdf]
      • [CARDS-56728]
        • Added a new check for the uniqueness of the "Tariff Code Ext" field (tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM) in a personal domain when approving a personal tariff. If several tariffs with the same "Tariff Code Ext" are found in the same personal tariff domain, an error message with the text "There is more than one tariff with TariffCodeExt = %%" will be returned.
        Upgrade Note:
        The system configuration must be checked using preliminary script for the presence of a non-unique value for the tariff.TABLE_CODE_FROM (Tariff Code Ext) field in the tariff domain. If this is the case, the codes must be given unique values.
        Check Scripts:
        CARDS-56728_TARIFF_table_code_from_uniqueness.sql
        Updated Manuals: [tariff_management\Tariff_Management.pdf]
